129. Provider usage live tool gained alert classification and proactive guidance on 2026-05-24. The core `FlowDeskProviderUsageCollectorResultV1` interface now carries an additive optional `bucketSnapshot` field (`resetBucket`, `remainingPercent`, `resetAt`, `uncertainty`) so consumers can read real remaining percentage without re-deriving it. `flowdesk_provider_usage_live` rows now expose `remainingPercent`, `alertLevel` (`ok`/`warning`/`critical`/`exhausted`/`stale`/`unknown`), and a short `recommendation` per provider, plus a top-level `worstAlertLevel` and `overallRecommendation` aggregate. Thresholds: >30%=ok, 10-30%=warning, >0-10%=critical, =0=exhausted; stale/unknown freshness or missing auth map to `stale`/`unknown`. Tool description was updated to instruct the assistant to PROACTIVELY call this tool before starting a large multi-step task that depends on a specific provider (extensive refactor, long agentic loop, multi-perspective review) and to surface the overallRecommendation when worstAlertLevel is critical or exhausted. Tests: a new `provider-usage-live-tool.test.ts` unit suite verifies per-row alertLevel/recommendation shape across all six levels and the blocked-no-provider-family path; server.test asserts description carries `ALSO PROACTIVELY USE`, `worstAlertLevel`, `alertLevel`, `recommendation`, `critical`, `exhausted`. Active OpenCode profile was repacked and force-reinstalled; live verification returned OpenAI `alertLevel=ok` with `remainingPercent=100` and a real reset_at, while Claude/Gemini stayed sanitized at `alertLevel=unknown` due to local auth absence, with `worstAlertLevel=unknown` and a clear `overallRecommendation` pointing at the missing-auth providers. Test count is now 485/485 passing. Authority flags remain unchanged: only the new diagnostic `providerUsageAcquired` flag is observable; dispatch/runtime/lane/fallback authority stays false.

133. Gemini Code Assist usage collector now reuses the cached `access_token` in `~/.gemini/oauth_creds.json` when it is still within the validity window, without requiring OAuth client id/secret refresh credentials. Implementation in `packages/core/src/provider-usage-collector.ts`: read `access_token` and `expiry_date` from the credentials file; if the cached token is non-empty and `expiry_date > observedAt + 5 minute margin`, use it directly for the `loadCodeAssist`/`retrieveUserQuota` API calls. Refresh path still runs when the cached token is expired AND `refresh_token` + client id/secret are all available. Fail-closed paths returns sanitized reasons: `gemini refresh token is missing`, `gemini oauth client evidence is missing and cached access token is expired`, or `gemini token refresh failed` depending on what is actually missing. Two new regression tests prove the cached-token path makes zero refresh calls and uses the cached Bearer token directly when expiry is in the future, and the expired-cached-token + no-client-id path returns the new sanitized `cached access token is expired` reason. Active OpenCode profile live verification with no `FLOWDESK_GEMINI_OAUTH_CLIENT_ID`/`SECRET` env vars now returns real Gemini Code Assist quota data: `alertLevel=ok`, `remainingPercent=100`, `resetBucket=gemini-flash-daily`, `resetTime=2026-05-25T09:49:55.000Z`. This makes the natural-language `사용량 보여줘` flow work out-of-the-box for users with the Gemini CLI installed and logged in, without needing to obtain or configure Gemini OAuth client id/secret. Test count is now 492/492 passing.
134. Claude macOS keychain auto-detection now works zero-config in the active OpenCode profile on 2026-05-24. The core `provider-usage-collector` keeps its `child_process` ban (Checkpoint 4 source safety contract: core source must not import `node:child_process` or contain `spawn`/`exec` calls); instead the plugin layer in `packages/opencode-plugin/src/provider-usage-live-tool.ts` now injects a `defaultExecFile` capability backed by `execFileSync` from `node:child_process`, with `stdio: ['ignore','pipe','ignore']` and utf-8 encoding, passed as `collectorOptions.execFile` when invoking `collectManagedDispatchBetaUsageEvidenceV1`. The Claude keychain credential read in the collector (`readClaudeKeychainCredentials` calling `/usr/bin/security find-generic-password` with the `Claude Code-credentials` service name) now succeeds out-of-the-box for users with Claude Code logged in via the keychain. Live verification in the active profile: Claude reports `alertLevel=ok`, `remainingPercent=86`, `resetBucket=claude-5h`; OpenAI reports `alertLevel=ok`, `remainingPercent=100`, `resetBucket=openai-gpt-5h`; Gemini reports `alertLevel=ok`, `remainingPercent=100`, `resetBucket=gemini-flash-daily`; `worstAlertLevel=ok` with `overallRecommendation` confirming all providers are dispatchable. This completes zero-config natural-language usage retrieval for all three concrete provider families (Claude OAuth via macOS keychain, OpenAI/Codex via ~/.codex/auth.json, Gemini Code Assist via cached access_token in ~/.gemini/oauth_creds.json). 136. Lane heartbeat stall projection contract was added to FlowDesk on 2026-05-24 covering FlowDesk-owned lanes only (reviewer lanes, runtime lane launches, provider acquisition lanes, managed-dispatch attempts, fallback regate plans). The implementation spec section `6.7a Lane Heartbeat and Stall Detection Contract` defines a 2-minute soft heartbeat interval, a 5-minute stall threshold, the heartbeat record contract, and the stall projection contract; `IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP.md` adds a Phase 1 task and `USER_MANUAL.md` exposes the classification in user terms. Core `packages/core/src/lane-stall-projection.ts` exports `projectFlowDeskLaneStallV1` which reads the latest `lane_lifecycle` entry per lane id from a `FlowDeskSessionEvidenceReloadResultV1` and classifies each lane as `progressing_normal` (<=2m since last signal), `progressing_late` (2m-5m), `stalled` (>5m while still in `created`/`running`), `terminal` (any of `complete`/`incomplete`/`no_output`/`missing_verdict`/`tool_calls_only_no_verdict`/`aborted`/`timeout`/`late_output`/`orphaned`/`invocation_failed`), or `unknown`. The result is a `flowdesk.lane_stall_projection.v1` shape carrying `observedAt`, `lateThresholdMs`, `stallThresholdMs`, totals per classification, a `worstClassification`, and per-lane entries with `seconds_since_last_signal`, `abnormal`, a `failureHint` derived from terminal states (e.g. `invocation_failed`, `transport_timeout`, `correlation_lost`, `abnormal_exit`), and a bounded `safeNextActions` allowlist limited to `/flowdesk-status`, `/flowdesk-retry`, `/flowdesk-resume`, `/flowdesk-abort`, `/flowdesk-doctor`, `/flowdesk-export-debug`. The minimum late threshold is clamped to 10 seconds and the stall threshold is always at least 1 second above it. Plugin `flowdesk_status_live` now consumes the projection per workflow and exposes `laneStallProjection`, `worstLaneStallClassification`, `stalledLaneCount`, `progressingLateLaneCount` per workflow plus a top-level `worstLaneStallClassification`, `totalStalledLaneCount`, and `totalProgressingLateLaneCount`. The tool description now explicitly triggers on natural-language stall phrases (English `is it stuck`, `stalled`, `no log`, `no update`, `no response`, `frozen`, `hung`, Korean `멈췄`, `멈춘 것 같`, `응답이 없`, `아무 로그도 없`, `진행이 안돼`, `먹통`) and instructs the assistant to surface stalled lanes without auto-retrying, auto-aborting, or auto-fallbacking. Chat routing in `packages/core/src/chat-routing.ts` recognizes the same Korean and English stall phrases and routes them to `/flowdesk-status`. Authority flags are unchanged: no new dispatch, fallback, or hard-chat authority. Tests now pass at 503/503 (seven new core projection tests, two new plugin status-live tests for the stall projection result and description vocabulary, one new chat-routing test for stalled-lane intents). Active OpenCode profile was repacked and force-reinstalled (`@flowdesk/core@0.1.0` and `@flowdesk/opencode-plugin@0.1.1` local tarballs); live smoke with one fresh lane and one stale lane returned `worstLaneStallClassification=stalled`, `totalStalledLaneCount=1`, `progressingLateLaneCount=0`, the stalled entry with `secondsSinceLastSignal=660`, and the safe next actions `/flowdesk-status`, `/flowdesk-retry`, `/flowdesk-resume`, `/flowdesk-abort`, `/flowdesk-doctor`, `/flowdesk-export-debug`. Default dispatch/runtime/lane/fallback/hard-chat authority remains unchanged and false.
137. Lane heartbeat evidence class, plugin writer tool, runtime reviewer hook, and chat.message stall alert card were added on 2026-05-24 (see `docs/conformance/2026-05-24-lane-stall-projection.md`). Core adds the `flowdesk.lane_heartbeat.v1` evidence class with states `created`, `running`, `awaiting_dependency`, `cooldown`, a `buildFlowDeskLaneHeartbeatRecordV1` helper that clamps `expectedIntervalMs` to >=10s and <=24h, a validator that rejects unknown properties, raw payload markers, authority smuggling, and `expected_next_heartbeat_at <= observed_at`; `lane-stall-projection.ts` now consumes heartbeat entries alongside lifecycle entries and chooses the latest signal per lane id, exposing `lastSignalSource`, `lastHeartbeatSeq`, and `expectedNextHeartbeatAt`. Plugin `flowdesk_lane_heartbeat_record` registers only when `laneHeartbeatWriter.enabled=true` and a durable state root resolves; it auto-increments `heartbeat_seq` per lane id from reloaded evidence, persists exactly one validated record per call, and returns `lane_heartbeat_recorded` with a `laneHeartbeatPersisted=true` diagnostic flag while keeping every dispatch/runtime/lane/fallback/hard-chat authority flag false. The runtime reviewer execution bridge writes a single launch-time heartbeat per reviewer lane right after `lane_launch_started`, before observing the typed reviewer verdict; failures stay diagnostic and do not block lane execution. Plugin `chat.message` now optionally appends a redacted stall alert card when `statusLive` and `chatMessageStallAlert` are both enabled and durable state has stalled lanes; the card lists stalled and progressing-late counts, top workflow ids with `last signal ~Xm ago` plus failure hints, the explicit `FlowDesk does not auto-retry, auto-abort, or auto-fallback on stall.` statement, and the full safe next action allowlist (`/flowdesk-status`, `/flowdesk-retry`, `/flowdesk-resume`, `/flowdesk-abort`, `/flowdesk-doctor`, `/flowdesk-export-debug`). Tests now pass at 510/510 with four new heartbeat unit tests plus a heartbeat-as-signal projection test, a plugin heartbeat writer registration/auto-seq test, and a chat.message stall alert card test. Active OpenCode profile was repacked and force-reinstalled; live verification recorded two heartbeats (seq=1, seq=2) for a synthetic lane that the status_live projection then classified as `progressing_normal` with `lastSignalSource=lane_heartbeat`; a separate live smoke with a stale lifecycle produced the chat.message stall card with the expected redacted lines. Default dispatch/runtime/lane/fallback/hard-chat authority remains unchanged and false; only `laneHeartbeatPersisted` and `statusEvidenceObserved` diagnostic flags can flip true.

157. FlowDesk-only active profile hardening was added on 2026-05-25 after raw OpenCode background tasks repeatedly appeared to stall outside FlowDesk durable lane monitoring. The active profile now sets `default_agent="flowdesk-main"` and has a global `agent/flowdesk-main.md` primary agent that routes ordinary work through FlowDesk tools first, treats raw background tasks as untracked unless their result-retrieval channel is available, and keeps task/bash/edit permissions at ask inside the agent profile. The Release 1 bootstrap installer now also materializes `agent/flowdesk-main.md` and updates `opencode.json.default_agent` during install, with rollback of both the agent file and config mutation if later durable bootstrap artifact writes fail. Targeted verification passed with `npm test --workspace @flowdesk/opencode-plugin -- --test-name-pattern "bootstrap installer|lane heartbeat|stall alert"` (172 selected tests) and an active installed-plugin smoke proving `flowdesk_lane_heartbeat_record` persists a stale synthetic heartbeat, `flowdesk_status_live` classifies it as `stalled` with the safe next-action allowlist, and `chat.message` appends the passive stall card without `noReply`, `cancel`, or `stop`. The investigation also confirmed the current heartbeat system is diagnostic and FlowDesk-owned-lane scoped: it writes explicit heartbeats or launch-time reviewer heartbeats, but it does not yet run a background 2-minute timer for arbitrary OpenCode background tasks and does not force-kill lanes after 5 minutes; forced termination remains intentionally unclaimed until a safe first-class OpenCode control surface is wired to FlowDesk-owned lane ids.

150. Optional repository-local code-graph MCP setup was migrated from `symgraph` to `codegraph` on 2026-05-26 for developer code exploration only. The prior `symgraph 2026.4.13` install (no automatic file-watcher; required manual `symgraph-reindex` calls) was uninstalled along with the empty `.symgraph/index.db`. `@colbymchenry/codegraph@0.9.4` is now installed locally under `.tools/codegraph/node_modules/`, with the platform binary `@colbymchenry/codegraph-darwin-arm64` resolved automatically. Initial `codegraph init -i` indexed 126 files into `.codegraph/codegraph.db` (8.5 MB, WAL+FTS5) producing 2,787 nodes and 11,714 edges in ~971ms. The FlowDesk project `opencode.json` now registers `codegraph` as a local MCP with `command: ["./.tools/codegraph/node_modules/.bin/codegraph", "serve", "--mcp", "--path", "."]`; `--path .` is required because watcher auto-sync silently misses changes when project root is left to client inference. `.gitignore` was updated from `.symgraph/` to `.codegraph/`, and `.tools/` continues to be ignored. Auto-sync was empirically verified: a probe file added at t=0 was searchable through `codegraph_search` at t≈2.5s, with stderr reporting `[CodeGraph MCP] Auto-synced 1 file(s) in 74ms`. The MCP server exposes 10 tools (`codegraph_search`, `codegraph_context`, `codegraph_callers`, `codegraph_callees`, `codegraph_impact`, `codegraph_node`, `codegraph_explore`, `codegraph_status`, `codegraph_files`, `codegraph_trace`). The watcher debounce window is hardcoded to 2000ms in `sync/watcher.js:75` and not forwarded from `mcp/index.js:377`; an upstream feature request for configurable debounce was filed at `https://github.com/colbymchenry/codegraph/issues/403`. This setup does not make codegraph a FlowDesk runtime dependency, registered FlowDesk tool, connector authority, evidence source, dispatch gate, provider/runtime/lane/fallback authority, or debug/audit persistence source; it is read-only developer tooling whose tools the assistant may call but whose output never enters FlowDesk authority paths.
149. `@flowdesk/core@0.1.4` and `@flowdesk/opencode-plugin@0.1.4` were published on the public npm registry on 2026-05-24, finishing the session-evidence shape validator dispatch gap surfaced by the spec-gap exploration. Session-evidence reload now dispatches to these for the matching evidence classes (`pre_dispatch_audit`, `usage_authority`, `runtime_echo`, `telemetry_correlation`). Shape-only validators are intentionally lenient — they only enforce schema_version equality and the redacted-raw-payload boundary — so that the full Release 2 cross-validation (usage snapshot match, conformance metadata, expected refs) keeps running at the higher dispatch path while the durable reload now also fails closed on schema_version drift and forbidden raw payloads. 143. `lane-stall-projection.ts` now surfaces heartbeat-declared overdue hints alongside the classification. Each per-lane entry can carry `expectedNextHeartbeatOverdue: boolean` and `secondsPastExpectedNextHeartbeat: number` when the projection's `observedAt` has crossed the heartbeat record's own `expected_next_heartbeat_at`. The classification itself still comes from the configurable `lateThresholdMs`/`stallThresholdMs` policy (default 2m/5m), so a lane that emitted a heartbeat with a 30-second expected interval but is only 90 seconds old still classifies as `progressing_normal` while reporting `expectedNextHeartbeatOverdue: true` as a diagnostic hint. One new core test (`stall projection flags expected_next_heartbeat_at as overdue when observed_at passes it`) asserts the hint flips true with `secondsPastExpectedNextHeartbeat > 0` while classification stays `progressing_normal`. Test count is now 513/513. Default dispatch/runtime/lane/fallback/hard-chat authority remains unchanged and false.

163. Quick reviewer typed-verdict prompt/schema alignment was fixed on 2026-05-26 after restarted exact-model lanes launched successfully but produced `missing_verdict` for Claude/Gemini and `invalid_verdict` for GPT. The root cause was not agent registration: lane lifecycle evidence showed `agent-reviewer-claude-opus`, `agent-reviewer-gpt-frontier`, and `agent-reviewer-gemini-pro` all launched with the intended concrete model ids. The issue was that `quickReviewerPrompt` embedded an invalid `flowdesk.top_tier_review_verdict.v1` template: finding objects used `summary` instead of `summary_label`, omitted `finding_id`, `evidence_refs`, and `required_fix_label`, and used invalid category `verification`. The prompt now emits a validator-clean template with `finding_id`, category `conformance`, `summary_label`, per-finding `evidence_refs`, and `required_fix_label`; it also derives `source` from the concrete reviewer binding (`claude_opus`, `gpt_frontier`, `gemini_pro`) instead of defaulting all lanes to `gpt_frontier`. Active profile reviewer prompts were strengthened to return exact typed JSON when requested, and `~/.config/opencode` was switched to local file dependencies for the rebuilt workspace packages so the fix will load after the next OpenCode restart. Verification passed with JSON syntax validation, `npm test --workspace @flowdesk/opencode-plugin -- --runInBand quick-reviewer-run` (175 selected plugin tests passing), and `git diff --check` on touched files. Existing in-memory sessions still need restart before the corrected plugin code is used. Dispatch/runtime/lane/fallback/hard-chat authority remains unchanged and false.

Status-live stall 오탐 1차 차단 패치가 2026-05-26에 적용되었습니다. `~/.flowdesk/.flowdesk/sessions/workflow-quick-reviewer-mpjndhgd/`에는 같은 lane(`lane-quick-verification_implementation-mpjndhgd` 등)에 대해 동일 `updated_at`을 갖는 `lifecycle-running-*`과 `lifecycle-complete-*` 페어가 모두 존재해 코어 `projectFlowDeskLaneStallV1`의 tie-breaker만으로는 `complete`이 항상 우선되지 않고, 일부 호출에서 `running` 신호가 5분 이상 정지로 분류돼 `worstClassification=stalled`가 반복 보고되는 회귀가 있었습니다. `packages/opencode-plugin/src/status-live-tool.ts`에 `pruneNonTerminalLifecycleSnapshotsNoLongerValid`를 추가해, 동일 lane에 동일 타임스탬프 또는 더 오래된 시점의 terminal lifecycle 레코드(`complete`, `aborted`, `timeout`, `invocation_failed` 등 10종)가 존재하면 그보다 같은 시점 이하의 비-terminal lifecycle 항목을 stall 프로젝션 입력에서 제외하고, projection에는 가공된 reload만 전달합니다. 회귀 테스트 `status live tool keeps terminal lifecycle when same-time running evidence is also present`가 추가됐고 전체 테스트 534/534 통과합니다. 코어 `lane-stall-projection`의 기존 우선순위/터미널 보정 로직은 그대로 유지되며, status-live 호출 경로에서만 가공이 일어납니다. 직접 require로 호출한 `executeFlowDeskStatusLiveV1`는 해당 워크플로우를 `terminal/0 stalled`로 분류함을 확인했지만, 현재 실행 중인 OpenCode 런타임에 로드된 플러그인 인메모리 모듈은 새 dist를 반영하지 못해 `flowdesk_status_live`는 여전히 `stalled` 보고를 계속하며 chat.message 스턴 카드도 사라지지 않습니다. 패치를 실사용에 반영하려면 OpenCode 재시작이 필요합니다. Stall recovery P4/P5 slice was added on 2026-05-26. `packages/opencode-plugin/src/stall-recovery.ts` now provides `validateAndAbortFlowDeskLaneEvidenceV1`, which can mark a FlowDesk-owned active lane as `aborted` by writing only a new `flowdesk.lane_lifecycle_record.v1` evidence record after workflow-prefix, lane ownership (`spawned_by=flowdesk` or legacy missing value), active-state, duplicate/terminal-state, schema, write, and reload verification checks. `/flowdesk-abort` now accepts optional `lane_id`; when supplied through the local non-dispatch adapter with a durable state root, the handler surfaces `cancel_observed` plus the lifecycle evidence ref while explicitly not calling SDK `session.abort`, not launching lanes, not making provider calls, and not claiming hard chat/no-reply authority. Non-FlowDesk-owned lanes, missing durable roots, disallowed workflow prefixes, missing lanes, terminal lanes, and write/reload failures block with redacted diagnostic reasons. P5 SDK-session-health diagnostics were also surfaced through `/flowdesk-doctor`: the compatibility section now includes `sdk_session_api_health`, `sdk_session_api_reason` when relevant, and `sdk_session_abort_automation=disabled_release1`; the local adapter reports `sdk_health_not_checked_non_dispatch_adapter` rather than implying a live SDK check. 168. Stall recovery P6 guarded auto-abort primitives were added on 2026-05-26 as an evidence-only hook-state-machine library, not as default Release 1 automatic cancellation. `packages/opencode-plugin/src/stall-recovery.ts` now defines `FlowDeskGuardSignOffV1`, RFC-8785-style deterministic canonical JSON, SHA-256 markdown digest checking, HMAC-SHA-256 sidecar verification (`verifyGuardSignOffHmacV1`), `computeGuardSignOffHmacV1` test helper, and `isAutoAbortEnabledV1`. The enablement gate fails closed unless `autoAbortOnStall=true`, a guard sign-off sidecar exists or is supplied, `p6_safe=true`, the markdown digest matches, the HMAC matches, the sign-off is unexpired, and a guard HMAC key is supplied; production mode rejects the environment-variable fallback key. `evaluateGuardedAutoAbortHookV1` implements the V10 hook-only matrix: disabled/missing Guard, non-confirmed stall, responsive/unknown SDK session health, or legacy ownership remain manual recommendation/no-op; confirmed explicit FlowDesk-owned stalls with `api_timeout` first write `flowdesk.pending_abort_warning.v1`; subsequent hook evaluations keep the warning pending until expiry, honor `flowdesk.pending_abort_cancel.v1` by writing a `cancelled` tombstone, and after expiry re-confirm by calling `validateAndAbortFlowDeskLaneEvidenceV1(requireExplicitOwnership=true)` then writing an `executed` tombstone. The path writes only pending-abort and lane-lifecycle evidence; it never calls SDK `session.abort`, never force-kills tasks, never launches lanes, never calls providers, and never claims hard chat/no-reply authority. Regression coverage now verifies HMAC/digest/expiry/env-production fail-closed behavior, warning issuance, pending state before expiry, evidence-only abort after expiry, and manual recommendation for disabled/responsive/legacy-owned cases. Verification passed with `npm run typecheck`, `npm run build --workspace @flowdesk/opencode-plugin`, and `node --test packages/opencode-plugin/dist/stall-recovery.test.js` (7/7). Full product wiring into a periodic hook remains intentionally not enabled by default; Release 1 user-facing safe actions remain `/flowdesk-status`, `/flowdesk-retry`, `/flowdesk-resume`, `/flowdesk-abort`, `/flowdesk-doctor`, and `/flowdesk-export-debug`.
169. P6 guarded auto-abort hook wiring was added on 2026-05-26 behind an explicit nested `chatMessageStallAlert.guardedAutoAbort` opt-in. The existing `chat.message` stall card path now parses `guardedAutoAbort` options (`autoAbortOnStall`, `preAbortWarningMs`, `guardSignOffPath`, `guardHmacKey`, `productionMode`, and bounded `sdkSessionHealth`) and, only when stalled lanes are already being surfaced by `statusLive`, calls `evaluateGuardedAutoAbortHookV1` for the primary stalled lane. The rendered stall card appends a redacted `Guarded auto-abort diagnostics (evidence-only, opt-in)` section showing per-workflow/lane statuses such as `warning_issued`, `warning_pending`, or `auto_abort_executed`. Default behavior is unchanged when the nested option is absent. The hook still emits a visible card only, never returns `noReply`/`cancel`/`stop`, and the auto-abort path still writes only `pending_abort_warning`/`pending_abort_cancel` tombstones and evidence-only `lane_lifecycle state=aborted`; it does not call SDK `session.abort`, force-kill tasks, launch lanes, call providers, retry, fallback, or promote dispatch/runtime/hard-chat authority. A new server regression seeds a FlowDesk-owned stalled lane, writes a signed Guard sidecar under the durable root, verifies the first chat hook call writes a pending warning and shows `guarded auto-abort warning_issued`, then advances the hook clock past `preAbortWarningMs` and verifies `guarded auto-abort auto_abort_executed`, persisted `lane_lifecycle state=aborted`, and a persisted `pending_abort_warning status=executed`. Verification passed with `npm run typecheck`, `npm run build --workspace @flowdesk/opencode-plugin`, and `node --test packages/opencode-plugin/dist/server.test.js --test-name-pattern "guarded auto-abort"` (70/70 selected server tests).
170. Active-profile guarded auto-abort was configured for actual use on 2026-05-26 with live SDK session-health checking rather than a static `api_timeout` test override. `packages/opencode-plugin/src/server.ts` now supports `chatMessageStallAlert.guardedAutoAbort.useLiveSdkSessionHealth=true`: when an injected OpenCode SDK client is present, the chat hook reloads the stalled lane lifecycle evidence to find the latest `parent_session_ref`, calls `checkSdkSessionApiHealthV1` via `session.messages`, and feeds the live result into the P6 state machine. If the parent session ref or SDK client is missing, the path fails closed as `unknown`/manual recommendation instead of warning or aborting. The active global OpenCode config at `~/.config/opencode/opencode.jsonc` was backed up to `opencode.jsonc.bak.pre-guarded-auto-abort-20260526`, then updated under the FlowDesk plugin tuple with `chatMessageStallAlert.guardedAutoAbort: { autoAbortOnStall: true, preAbortWarningMs: 60000, productionMode: true, useLiveSdkSessionHealth: true, guardHmacKey: <local secret> }`. The matching Guard ADR sidecar was written under the durable root at `~/.flowdesk/docs/adr/0002-sdk-surface-verification.md` and `~/.flowdesk/docs/adr/0002-sdk-surface-verification.guard_sign_off.json`, signed with a locally generated HMAC key that was not printed in logs or docs. A direct plugin-load smoke confirmed JSON validity, Guard enablement, live-health option presence, 15 registered tools, and `chat.message` hook registration. Full verification after the live-health wiring passed with `npm test` (550/550) and `git diff --check`. The running OpenCode process must be restarted before the active-profile config and rebuilt local plugin code are used.

165. Stall Recovery V2 독립 설계 문서가 2026-05-26에 추가되었습니다. V1 계획(`docs/STALL_RECOVERY_PLAN.md`)은 3-perspective 다관점 리뷰(Claude Opus: blocked, Gemini Pro: changes_required, GPT Frontier: changes_required)에서 (1) OMO 소스 의존 위반(Safety Rule 1), (2) P3 자동 fallback chain이 Release 1 금지 범위 위반, (3) Guard 승인 없는 auto-abort, (4) 거버넌스 역전(구현 전 rule 10 선행 수정 제안), (5) client.event.subscribe API 부재로 P0 event-watchdog 전제 미성립 등 critical 결함으로 blocked 판정을 받았습니다. FlowDesk 코드베이스 탐색을 통해 실제 SDK 표면(`client.session.abort/messages/children` 존재, `client.event.*` 미존재), 현재 stall 감지 방식(chat.message hook 발화 시 on-demand polling, background timer 없음), collectStallAlertSummary timeout 없음 등을 확인했습니다. `docs/STALL_RECOVERY_PLAN_V2.md`는 OMO 코드 전혀 없이 독립 재설계로 P1(withTimeout helper, FlowDeskTimeoutError, conservative defaults), P2(SDK 스파이크 — session.abort/messages 동작 사전 검증, ADR 작성), P3(collectStallAlertSummary에 withTimeout wrapping, statusLiveTimeoutMs 설정 노출), P4(Lane Abort Tool — FlowDesk evidence only, SDK 세션과 분리), P5(Session Health Check, P2 검증 조건부), P6(Guarded Auto-Abort, multi-factor 판정, default false, Guard 연계)를 정의합니다. OMO 상수 하드코딩 없음, P3 fallback chain 제거, auto-abort는 confirmed_stall 다중 조건 + abortOnlyFlowDeskOwnedLanes 보호, rule 10은 구현·테스트·ADR 완료 후에만 수정합니다. 코드 변경 없음(설계 문서만 추가). Dispatch/runtime/lane/fallback/hard-chat authority 미변경.

173. P7 Guarded Auto-Retry steps 1–7 were implemented on 2026-05-26. `packages/core/src/retry-plan.ts` was created with four evidence interfaces (`FlowDeskReviewerLaneContextV1`, `FlowDeskPendingRetryPlanV1`, `FlowDeskRetryExecutedV1`, `FlowDeskRetryFailedV1`), `DisabledAutoRetryReason` union, `FlowDeskAutoRetryResultV1` union, and four closed validators following the `pending-abort.ts` pattern. `state-paths.ts` gained four new evidence class segments (`reviewer_lane_context`, `pending_retry_plan`, `retry_executed`, `retry_failed`) and matching path strings. `session-evidence.ts` imports the four new validators and dispatches to them in `validateEvidenceShape`; `EVIDENCE_SCHEMA_BY_CLASS` maps the four new classes to their schema versions. `packages/core/src/index.ts` re-exports `retry-plan.ts`. `runtime-reviewer-execution-bridge.ts` now writes `reviewer_lane_context.v1` evidence immediately after lane-launch heartbeat (SHA-256 of full prompt, 8192-char truncation, redaction_version `v1`); the write is wrapped in try/catch and never fails the lane launch. `stall-recovery.ts` gained: `FlowDeskAutoAbortConfigV1.autoRetryAfterAbort` and `maxAutoRetries` optional fields; `reconcileStalePendingRetryPlansV1` which marks `pending_retry_plan(launched)` records older than 10 minutes without terminal evidence as `retry_failed(indeterminate_launch)`; and `evaluateGuardedAutoRetryHookV1` implementing the 15-step execution order from the design doc (opt-in check, Guard HMAC re-verify, SDK client check with `retry_failed(sdk_unavailable)` evidence write, context load, redaction check, workflow/perspective invariant check, cap counting across retry_executed+retry_failed+pending(pending|launched), concurrent-retry fence, monotonic aborted-lifecycle check, new lane id allocation, `pending_retry_plan(pending)` idempotency fence write before SDK call, SDK launch with 30s timeout, failure-category differentiation sdk_create_failed/sdk_prompt_rejected, and success path writing retry_executed+pending→launched). `server.ts` parses `autoRetryAfterAbort` and `maxAutoRetries` (clamped 1–2) from `guardedAutoAbort` plugin config; calls `reconcileStalePendingRetryPlansV1` for each stalled workflow in the stall alert handler; calls `evaluateGuardedAutoRetryHookV1` after `auto_abort_executed` when `autoRetryAfterAbort=true`; and appends retry status to the stall card diagnostics. Verification: `npm run typecheck` (zero errors), `npm run build --workspace @flowdesk/opencode-plugin` (passes), `npm test` (550/550). All existing tests still pass. Dispatch/runtime/lane/fallback/hard-chat authority remains unchanged and false; auto-retry fires only through the same developer-mode injected-SDK path as `flowdesk_quick_reviewer_run` and requires explicit Guard HMAC re-verification per attempt.

172. Quick reviewer subset acceptance blocker가 2026-05-26에 수정되었습니다. Live smoke에서 Gemini preview 단일 `verification_implementation` lane은 launch/verdict/materialization evidence가 모두 성공했지만 `prepareFlowDeskReviewerTypedVerdictAcceptanceAdapterV1`가 항상 canonical 3-perspective verdict set만 요구해 `acceptedPerspectives=[]`, `blocked_before_acceptance`, `blocked_before_durable_acceptance`로 막히는 문제가 확인되었습니다. `prepareFlowDeskReviewerTypedVerdictAcceptanceAdapterV1`와 `prepareFlowDeskDurableReviewerVerdictLinkageAdapterV1`에 optional `requiredPerspectives`를 추가했고, 명시된 requested subset이 있을 때는 canonical perspective membership, distinct requested perspectives, consumed `reviewer_fanout` approval, pass/low-uncertainty verdict, workflow/attempt alignment, non-empty evidence refs, duplicate verdict/perspective 차단, unrequested perspective 차단, exact requested count를 모두 검증한 뒤 해당 subset만 accept/link합니다. 기존 호출처럼 `requiredPerspectives`가 없으면 이전 strict canonical 3-perspective promotion path를 그대로 사용하므로 full acceptance semantics는 약화하지 않았습니다. `executeFlowDeskRuntimeReviewerExecutionBridgeV1`는 실제 `verdictExpectations`에서 requested perspectives를 전달해 quick reviewer single/subset runs가 성공한 durable verdict를 acceptance/linkage까지 진행할 수 있게 했습니다. Regression coverage: `reviewer typed verdict acceptance adapter accepts explicit requested subset`, `durable reviewer verdict linkage adapter links explicit requested subset`, and integrated quick reviewer helper test `quick reviewer run completes a requested single-perspective subset`, which drives fake SDK create/prompt/messages through launch, observation, verdict materialization, durable lifecycle, subset acceptance, durable linkage, and `summaryForUser`. Verification: `npm run typecheck` 통과, targeted quick reviewer/watchdog tests pass, full `npm test -- --silent` 573/573 pass. 권한 경계는 unchanged: typed-verdict acceptance and durable linkage still do not promote real dispatch/provider/runtime/lane/fallback/hard-chat authority.

Agent task runner model-id/runtime response compatibility fix was added on 2026-05-26 after live `flowdesk_agent_task_run` attempts showed two failures: `anthropic/claude-opus-4-7` was rejected as `model id provider family is not dispatchable`, and `openai/gpt-5.5` launched but returned `task_failed(no_response)` because `agent-task-runner.ts` queried `session.messages` only with the legacy `{ path: { id } }` shape and only scanned top-level arrays/`items`. Core `validateProviderQualifiedModelId` now accepts actual OpenCode runtime provider prefixes `anthropic` and `google` in addition to FlowDesk families (`claude`, `gemini`, `openai`, etc.), while the runtime adapter maps `anthropic -> anthropic` and `google -> google` alongside the existing `claude -> anthropic` / `gemini -> google` aliases. `executeFlowDeskAgentTaskV1` now reads messages with the current `{ sessionID }` SDK shape first, falls back to legacy `{ path: { id } }` only on SDK error, and extracts assistant text from arrays, `data.items`, or `data.messages`, including messages where role is under `info.role`. Regression coverage added provider-id validation for `anthropic/...` and `google/...`, updated the agent-task execution test to use `anthropic/claude-opus-4-7`, and added a current-SDK messages-shape test returning `data.messages`. The running OpenCode process must be restarted to load the rebuilt plugin; before restart the old in-memory tool can still report `task_failed(no_response)`.

180. Usage auto-refresh on stale chat input was added on 2026-05-27. The `chat.message` hook now triggers `flowdesk_provider_usage_live` automatically on any user prompt if the existing sidebar usage cache is missing or older than 3 minutes. This keeps the provider usage display up to date when the user is active, without relying on continuous background polling.

181. Workflow orchestration tools were added on 2026-05-27 completing the planner layer of the natural-language to multi-task execution pipeline. `executeFlowDeskWorkflowAuthorToolV1` calls an agent once to decompose a `goalSummary` into a validated task DAG and writes `workflow_authoring_result.v1` and `task_graph.v1` evidence. `executeFlowDeskWorkflowAssignToolV1` reads the task graph and current provider usage sidebar cache, applies usage/fit scoring, and writes `task_agent_assignment.v1` and `task_model_selection.v1` evidence per task without calling providers or opening dispatch authority. `executeFlowDeskWorkflowSynthesisToolV1` reads completed `task_result.v1` evidence, calls an agent once to produce a redacted synthesis, and writes `workflow_synthesis_result.v1` evidence. All three tools preserve Release 1 non-dispatch authority constraints. Full `npm test` 668/668 and build passed.

 182. `executeFlowDeskWorkflowOrchestratorV1` was added on 2026-05-27 as the top-level 4-step pipeline connector. It chains Author → Assign (reads provider usage sidebar) → Schedule (DAG execution via existing scheduler) → Synthesize into a single call, propagating evidence between steps through durable session evidence, failing closed at each step with `summaryForUser` and `safeNextActions`, and keeping all authority flags false throughout. It is exposed as an opt-in `flowdesk_orchestrate` MCP tool behind `workflowOrchestrate.enabled=true` and `workflowOrchestrate.devBetaActualLaneLaunch=true`, requiring per-call `developerModeAcknowledged=true`, `allowProviderCall=true`, and `allowActualLaneLaunch=true`. Full `npm test` 668/668 and build passed.

183. Completion cache terminalization was strengthened on 2026-05-29 for failed/aborted task recovery paths so the subtask activity sidebar no longer shows stale running entries. `monitorChildSessionsV1` now refreshes completion UI caches when child-session writes fail and when lane launch fails (`sdk_create_failed`), and `async-lane.test.ts` added coverage for launch-failed terminalization plus strengthened abort cache assertions (`state="invocation_failed"` + `classification="terminal"`). Verified in this session with `npm run build && node --test packages/opencode-plugin/dist/async-lane.test.js`, `node --test packages/opencode-plugin/dist/server.test.js`, and targeted plugin regression tests; all ran clean.

184. Lifecycle-only terminal lane UI promotion was fixed on 2026-05-30. Before the fix, `refreshFlowDeskCompletionUiCachesV1` only derived terminal rows from `task_result` or `task_failed` evidence; a lane that reached terminal state via `lane_lifecycle` alone (e.g., reviewer execution bridge writing only `lane_lifecycle=invocation_failed` with no `task_failed` companion) appeared stuck at `state="running"` / `classification="progressing_normal"` in the subtask activity sidebar even though the lane was actually terminal. `completion-ui-cache.ts` now picks up the latest terminal `lane_lifecycle` per lane (states: `complete`, `invocation_failed`, `no_output`, `incomplete`, `aborted`, `timeout`) and promotes lifecycle-only failures to `classification="terminal"`, `progressPhase="failed"`, and the failed recovery action set (`/flowdesk-retry`, `/flowdesk-resume`, `/flowdesk-abort`, `/flowdesk-status`, `/flowdesk-export-debug`). The `ready` aggregation still requires `state==="task_result"` so lifecycle-only failed lanes correctly do NOT mark a workflow auto-next-ready. `stall-recovery.ts` (`monitorChildSessionsV1`) was tightened to always invoke the UI cache refresh for terminal lanes lacking `task_result` evidence — the previously-dead `terminalTaskResultLaneIds` set is now used to bypass the per-cycle dedup for those cases, guaranteeing each lifecycle-only terminal gets a refresh pass. A regression test (`monitorChildSessions promotes UI row to terminal when lane has only lane_lifecycle invocation_failed (no task_result, no task_failed)`) writes a lifecycle-only `invocation_failed` record and asserts the sidebar row becomes `state="invocation_failed"` + `classification="terminal"` + failed recovery actions, while auto-next-ready remains empty. Verification: `npm run build`, `node --test packages/opencode-plugin/dist/async-lane.test.js` (17/17 pass), `node --test packages/opencode-plugin/dist/completion-ui-cache.test.js` (3/3 pass), `node --test packages/opencode-plugin/dist/stall-recovery.test.js` (24/24 pass), `node --test packages/opencode-plugin/dist/server.test.js` (97/97 pass), plus managed-dispatch-adapter (61/61), quick-reviewer-run/index/commands/auto-continue/command-handlers batch (38/38 partial sample), status-live-tool (7/7), tui-subtask-activity (11/11), workflow-synthesis-tool (1/1). All runtime/dispatch/lane/fallback/hard-chat authority flags remain false.

185. Terminal/failure completion-cache recovery was hardened on 2026-05-30 for Release-1-safe paths. `refreshFlowDeskCompletionUiCachesV1` now uses timestamp-selected evidence per lane, monotonic cache `observed_at` handling, idempotent row/workflow merges, and lane-keyed row replacement so duplicate or out-of-order `invocation_failed`, `no_output`, `task_failed`, and late context signals cannot regress a terminal sidebar row or stale auto-next readiness. `event-hook-observer.ts` refreshes completion UI caches after `session.error` terminal evidence, and `backfillTerminalAgentTaskFailedLanesV1` refreshes even when only failure evidence exists and no `task_result` was written. Regression coverage in `completion-ui-cache.test.ts` now covers failure/no-output without task_result, event-order inversion, and duplicate terminal signals. Verified with `npm run typecheck && node --test packages/opencode-plugin/dist/completion-ui-cache.test.js` (6/6). No runtime dispatch, provider/fallback, policy, write/apply, or hard-chat authority was added.
